progress through partitions. The implementation spans multiple layers:\\n\\n### Core Offset Storage and Management\\n\\n**OffsetAndMetadata** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489) exists in two forms:\\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java**: The client-side representation used by consumer applications to commit and track offsets\\n- **group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java**: The server-side representation stored in the __consumer_offsets topic with additional metadata like commit timestamp and leader epoch\\n\\n**OffsetMetadataManager** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is the central component that manages all offset operations. It:\\n- Maintains mappings from group ID to topic-partition to offset metadata\\n- Implements offset commit handling via `commitOffsets()` method\\n- Validates offset fetch/commit requests through `validateOffsetFetch()` and `validateOffsetCommit()` methods\\n- Handles offset expiry and cleanup through the `cleanupExpiredOffsets()` method\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Retention\\n\\nOffset expiration is controlled by the **OffsetExpirationCondition** interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java) with implementation in **OffsetExpirationConditionImpl** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java). The `isOffsetExpired()` method determines when an offset should be removed based on configurable retention time.\\n\\nThe __consumer_offsets topic itself uses log compaction for cleanup. **LogCleaner** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleaner.java) and **LogCleanerManager** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java) handle the compaction of offset records, ensuring duplicate keys are removed while maintaining the latest offset state. **CleanerConfig** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/CleanerConfig.java) controls log cleanup policies and retention parameters.\\n\\n### Coordinator Architecture\\n\\n**GroupCoordinator** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) is the interface defining the contract for group coordination. The actual implementation is split:\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorService** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java): The service layer that handles API requests for offset operations. It implements `commitOffsets()`, `fetchOffsets()`, and `fetchAllOffsets()` methods that coordinate with group-specific shards.\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorShard** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java): The shard layer that manages state for a subset of groups. It coordinates between GroupMetadataManager and OffsetMetadataManager, implementing the actual offset fetch/commit logic.\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorConfig** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java): Configuration parameters for coordinator behavior including offsets topic settings, retention periods, and group timeout values.\\n\\n### Group Type Specific Handling\\n\\nDifferent group types handle offsets differently through the **Group** interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/Group.java) which defines `validateOffsetCommit()` and `validateOffsetFetch()` methods. Implementations include:\\n\\n- **ClassicGroup** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java): The original consumer group protocol with simple offset management\\n- **ConsumerGroup** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java): The modern KIP-848 group protocol with enhanced offset tracking\\n- **StreamsGroup** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/StreamsGroup.java): Kafka Streams-specific group handling\\n- **ShareGroup** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroup.java): Share consumer group implementation\\n\\n### Request Protocol Implementation\\n\\n**OffsetCommit Request/Response** are implemented in:\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitRequest.java\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitResponse.java\\n\\nThese handle the client-side protocol for committing offsets.\\n\\n**OffsetFetch Request/Response** are implemented in:\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchRequest.java\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchResponse.java\\n\\nThese handle fetching committed offsets for consumers.\\n\\n**TxnOffsetCommit Request/Response** are implemented in:\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/TxnOffsetCommitRequest.java\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/TxnOffsetCommitResponse.java\\n\\nThese handle transactional offset commits for exactly-once semantics.\\n\\n### Client-Side Coordination\\n\\nThe client-side consumer implementation includes:\\n- **CommitRequestManager** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java): Manages offset commit requests for the consumer\\n- **ConsumerCoordinator** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerCoordinator.java): Coordinates with the broker for group operations including offset management\\n- **OffsetCommitCallback** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetCommitCallback.java): Interface for asynchronous commit callbacks\\n- **OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker.java): Invokes registered commit callbacks\\n- **OffsetCommitMetricsManager** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/metrics/OffsetCommitMetricsManager.java): Tracks metrics for offset commit operations\\n\\n### Support Infrastructure\\n\\n**GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java) provides utility methods for creating coordinator records in the __consumer_offsets topic.\\n\\n**Topic** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/internals/Topic.java) defines the constant for the __consumer_offsets internal topic name.\\n\\n**GroupCoordinatorMetrics** and **GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard** (in the metrics subpackage) track performance metrics for offset operations and group coordination.\\n\\n### Offset Cleanup and Compaction\\n\\nThe __consumer_offsets topic is configured with cleanup.policy=compact,delete to maintain offset history. The LogCleaner component periodically compacts the topic, removing obsolete offset records while preserving the latest state. Offset records are also deleted after the configured retention period (default 1 day) to prevent unbounded growth. The implementation spans multiple layers:\\n\\n### Core Offset Storage and Management\\n\\n**OffsetAndMetadata** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489) exists in two forms:\\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java**: The client-side representation used by consumer applications to commit and track offsets\\n- **group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java**: The server-side representation stored in the __consumer_offsets topic with additional metadata like commit timestamp and leader epoch\\n\\n**OffsetMetadataManager** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is the central component that manages all offset operations. The `isOffsetExpired()` method determines when an offset should be removed based on configurable retention time.\\n\\nThe __consumer_offsets topic itself uses log compaction for cleanup. **LogCleaner** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleaner.java) and **LogCleanerManager** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java) handle the compaction of offset records, ensuring duplicate keys are removed while maintaining the latest offset state. **CleanerConfig** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/CleanerConfig.java) controls log cleanup policies and retention parameters.\\n\\n### Coordinator Architecture\\n\\n**GroupCoordinator** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) is the interface defining the contract for group coordination. It implements `commitOffsets()`, `fetchOffsets()`, and `fetchAllOffsets()` methods that coordinate with group-specific shards.\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorShard** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java): The shard layer that manages state for a subset of groups. It coordinates between GroupMetadataManager and OffsetMetadataManager, implementing the actual offset fetch/commit logic.\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorConfig** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java): Configuration parameters for coordinator behavior including offsets topic settings, retention periods, and group timeout values.\\n\\n### Group Type Specific Handling\\n\\nDifferent group types handle offsets differently through the **Group** interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/Group.java) which defines `validateOffsetCommit()` and `validateOffsetFetch()` methods. management\\n- **ConsumerGroup** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java): The modern KIP-848 group protocol with enhanced offset tracking\\n- **StreamsGroup** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/StreamsGroup.java): Kafka Streams-specific group handling\\n- **ShareGroup** Coordination\\n\\nThe client-side consumer implementation includes:\\n- **CommitRequestManager** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java): Manages offset commit requests for the consumer\\n- **ConsumerCoordinator** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerCoordinator.java): Coordinates with the broker for group
